## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (rate laws / concentration ODE models)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is explicitly the time-derivative of a chemical concentration A(t), which is the standard object of ordinary-differential-equation (ODE) reaction-rate modeling. With only t and A available, the most likely relationships are autonomous/nonautonomous rate laws where the reaction rate depends on concentration, possibly with time-varying rate coefficients or approach-to-equilibrium terms.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 (constant-rate depletion, e.g., surface-limited or saturated catalyst)
- First-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay, radioactive-like kinetics, many elementary steps under pseudo-first-order conditions)
- Nth-order (power-law) rate: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical rate order from data fitting)
- Second-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular/self-reaction or second-order in A approximation)
- Approach to equilibrium (linear relaxation): dA_dt = -c0 * (A - c1) (reversible reaction near equilibrium with A_eq = c1)
- Source-plus-decay (open system / feed term): dA_dt = c0 - c1 * A (constant production with first-order loss)
- Autocatalytic / logistic-type kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-accelerating production with limiting capacity/stoichiometric cap)
- Inhibited (self-limiting) rate: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (c1 * A + 1) (rate decreases at high A due to inhibition/transport limits)
- Rational (generalized saturation in A): dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 / (A**c1 + c2) (empirical saturation of the effective order in A)
- Time-varying first-order coefficient: dA_dt = -c0 * exp(c1 * t) * A (nonautonomous kinetics with accelerating/decelerating effective rate constant)
- Drifted rate coefficient: dA_dt = -c0 * (1 + c1 * t) * A (slow linear change in effective rate constant over time)
- Periodically driven kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * A (light/pulse-driven or oscillatory environmental forcing)
- Polynomial rate expansion: dA_dt = c0 + c1 * A + c2 * A**2 (local approximation to more complex mechanisms or truncated series model)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Elementary depletion mechanisms usually imply dA_dt ≤ 0 for A ≥ 0, so structures like -c*A, -c*A^n, or -c are common sign constraints.
- If the rate slows as A decreases (typical depletion), the magnitude |dA_dt| often scales with A or A^n; near A≈0, rates tend to 0 for n>0.
- Reversible reactions or relaxation-to-steady-state often appear as linear dependence on the deviation from an equilibrium/steady value: dA_dt ∝ -(A - A_eq).
- Autocatalysis/self-activation yields small rates at low A, faster mid-range growth/consumption, and eventual slowdown due to depletion/limits, captured by A*(c - A) or higher-order polynomials.
- Transport limitation or inhibition can make the effective rate increase sublinearly with A and then flatten, suggesting rational forms like A/(1+c*A) or A^n/(A^n+c).
- Time-varying experimental conditions (mixing, illumination, catalyst deactivation) produce nonautonomous coefficients k(t), motivating k(t)*A with k(t) as exp(c*t), (1+c*t), or sinusoidal modulation.
- Open systems (feed/removal) often require an additive source/sink offset, giving affine-in-A forms such as c0 - c1*A that admit nonzero steady states.
- When the mechanism is unknown, a low-order polynomial in A for dA_dt is a common surrogate that can approximate multiple regimes (initial transient vs later-time decay).

Best expression     : A*c0 + A + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + A**c4*c5*exp(c6*t)
Structure desc      : Sum of a linear baseline A*(1+c0) plus two decaying-in-t power laws in A (each A**ci multiplied by exp(·t)). A enters as A, A**c1 and A**c4, while t enters only via exp(c3*t) and exp(c6*t). Numerically, A*(1+c0)=0.3429A and the extra terms are ≈(-3.768)A^1.162 e^{-0.0774 t} + (2.514)A^1.090 e^{-0.208 t}, so behavior is a linear trend with two decaying corrections of opposite sign.

============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK21)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_q*A*log(c3*t + c4)
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed bivariate function
\[
F(t,A)=A\Big(0.08820105614498638\;\log(0.4381050266935539\,t+1)\;-\;0.9112380846295999\,e^{-0.08901020540483869\,t}\Big).
\]
Key structural facts that must hold for any equivalent candidate (for all real \(A,t\) in the common domain \(t>-1/0.4381\)):

1) **Overall linear in \(A\)**: \(F(t,A)=A\cdot g(t)\). No \(A^2\), no \(|A|\), no \(\cos(A\cdot)\), no \(e^{A\cdot}\), no \(\log(A\cdot)\), no rational-in-\(A\) factors, etc., unless they can be parameter-set to reduce exactly to \(A\cdot g(t)\).

2) **\(t\)-dependence includes a log term**: \(g(t)\) contains \(\log(\alpha t+1)\) with \(\alpha\neq 0\). So any matching candidate must be able to produce an \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\) term. None of the candidates have \(\log(\text{linear in }t)\) multiplied by \(A\); the only logs present are \(\log(A\cdot +1)\) or \(\log(c7*exp(A*c8)+1)\), i.e., logs depending on \(A\), not \(t\).

3) **Also includes a decaying exponential in \(t\)**: \(-0.9112\,A\,e^{-0.08901 t}\). Many candidates can produce an \(A\exp(c t)\) term by setting exponent parameters, but they still must also produce the \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\) term.

Given (2), we can already anticipate no match; below is a candidate-by-candidate check.

---

### 1. `A*c0 + A + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + A**c4*c5*exp(c6*t)`
Only polynomial/exponential-in-\(t\) terms; no \(\log(\text{linear in }t)\). Cannot match GT.  

### 2. `A*A**c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + A**c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*log(A*c8 + 1)`
Has \(\log\) but it is \(\log(A\cdot+1)\) (depends on \(A\)), not \(\log(\alpha t+1)\). Also other terms are exponentials/powers. Cannot match.  

### 3. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t)*cos(A*c4) + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7`
Contains \(\cos(A\cdot)\) and an \(A\)-independent exponential term \(c5 e^{c6 t}\) unless forced to 0. Even if set \(c4=0\) so \(\cos(0)=1\) and kill \(c5\), still no \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). Cannot match.  

### 4. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A**c3*c4*exp(c5*t)*cos(A*c6)`
Again only exponentials in \(t\) and possible \(\cos(A\cdot)\); no \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). Cannot match.  

### 5. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*t + c7))`
Has a non-log nonlinear \(t\) term \(exp(sin(\cdot))\) and no \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). Cannot match.  

### 6. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3 + c4*exp(A**c5*c6*exp(c7*t))`
Has \(A\) inside an exponential; GT is linear in \(A\). Even if that term is killed, no \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). Cannot match.  

### 7. `A*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/(c3*exp(c4*t) + 1) + A + A**c5*c6*exp(c7*t) + c8`
Only rational/exponential in \(t\); no log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 8. `A*c0 + A*c1 + A + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*t/(c6*t + c7) + c8/(c6*t + c7) + c9`
Has rational-in-\(t\) terms not multiplied by \(A\), and no \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). Cannot match.  

### 9. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*Abs(A) + c5*exp(c6*sin(c7*t + c8)) + c9`
Contains \(|A|\) and non-log \(t\) dependence; cannot reduce to \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\) term. Cannot match.  

### 10. `A*c0 + A + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + A**c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + A**c7*c8*cos(c9*t)`
No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 11. `A*c0 + A*c1 + A + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8) + 1)`
Log depends on \(A\), not \(t\). Cannot match.  

### 12. `A*A**c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + A*c4 + c5 + c6*exp(A*c7) + c8*exp(A*c9)`
Has \(e^{A\cdot}\) terms; GT linear in \(A\). No \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). Cannot match.  

### 13. `A*c0 + A*c1/(c2*t + c3) + A*c4/(A*c5 + 1) + c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8 + c9/(c2*t + c3)`
Has \(\log(A\cdot)\) and rational terms; no \(\log(\alpha t+1)\). Also has nonlinearity in \(A\) via \(A/(A c5+1)\) unless killed. Cannot match.  

### 14. `A*c0 + 2*A + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*Abs(A)**c5/(c6 + Abs(A)**c5) + c7`
Has \(|A|\)-based saturation term; no log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 15. `A*c0*exp(A*c1) + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t)`
Nonlinear in \(A\) via \(A e^{A c1}\) unless \(c1=0\) (then becomes \(A c0\)), still no \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). Cannot match.  

### 16. `A*c0 + A*c1/(A*c2 + 1) + A**c3*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6`
Has rational-in-\(A\) term; can be killed by \(c1=0\), but still only exponential-in-\(t\), no \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). Cannot match.  

### 17. `A*A**c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + c4*exp(A*c5) + c6*exp(A*c7) + c8`
Has \(e^{A\cdot}\) terms; no \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). Cannot match.  

### 18. `A*c0*exp(A*c1) + A*c2 + A**c3*c4*exp(c5*t)`
Even if \(c1=0\) to linearize, still lacks \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). Cannot match.  

### 19. `A*c0 + 2*A + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + A**c4*c5/(A**c4 + c6)`
Has nonlinear rational-in-\(A\) term; no log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 20. `A*A**c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + c4`
No log-in-\(t\); also constant term \(c4\) must be 0 but still no log. Cannot match.  

### 21. `A*c0 + 2*A + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4`
No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 22. `A*c0 + A*c1 + A + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5`
No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 23. `A*A**c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + c4*exp(A*c5) + c6`
Has \(e^{A\cdot}\); no log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 24. `A*c0 + A + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t)`
No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 25. `A*c0 + A*c1 + 2*A + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t)`
No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 26. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t)`
No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 27. `A*c0 + A*c1 + A + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t)`
No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 28. `A*c0 + 2*A + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t)`
No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 29. `A*c0 + A*c1 + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*log(A*c6 + 1)`
Log depends on \(A\), not \(t\). Cannot match.  

### 30. `A*c0 + A*c1 + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*t*(A + c6)**c7`
Introduces \(t\cdot(A+c6)^{c7}\) coupling; cannot become \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). Cannot match.  

### 31. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*Abs(A)`
Has \(|A|\) term; no log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 32. `A*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + A**c3*c4*exp(c5*t)`
No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 33. `A*c0 + 2*A + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*t/(c5*t + c6) + c7/(c5*t + c6)`
Rational-in-\(t\) terms not of log form and not multiplied by \(A\). Cannot match.  

### 34. `A*c0 + 2*A + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*log(A*c5 + 1)`
Log depends on \(A\), not \(t\). Cannot match.  

### 35. `A*c0 + A*c1 + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t)`
No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 36. `A*c0 + 2*A + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(A*c5) + c6`
Has \(e^{A\cdot}\); no log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 37. `A*c0 + 2*A + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*Max(0, A)`
Nonlinear piecewise in \(A\); no log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 38. `A*A**c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + c4*Abs(A) + c5`
Has \(|A|\) and no log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 39. `A*A**c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + A*c4 + c5`
No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 40. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t)*cos(A*c4) + c5`
Even if \(c4=0\) to remove cosine dependence, still no log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 41. `A*c0 + 2*A + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6*Abs(A)**c7/(c8 + Abs(A)**c7) + c9`
Log depends on \(A\), plus \(|A|\)-nonlinearity; no log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 42. `A*A**c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3`
No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 43. `A + A**c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + A**c3*c4 + A**c3*c5*t + c6*t/(c7*t + c8) + c9/(c7*t + c8)`
No log-in-\(t\); also includes \(A^p\) terms and \(A^p t\). Cannot match.  

### 44. `A*A**c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + c4*log(A*c5 + 1)`
Log depends on \(A\), not \(t\). Cannot match.  

### 45. `A*c0 + A*c1 + A + A**c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*log(A*c6 + 1) + c7`
Log depends on \(A\), not \(t\). Cannot match.  

### 46. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t)*cos(A*c4)`
No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 47. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + A*c4*t + c5 + c6*exp(A**c7*c8*exp(c9*t))`
Has \(A t\) term and \(A\) inside an exponential; no log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 48. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A + A**c3*c4*exp(c5*t) + A**c6*c7*exp(c8*t)`
Sum of \(A\)-scaled exponentials/powers; no log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 49. `A**2*c0 + A*c1*exp(A*c2) + A*c3 + A*c4 + A**c5*c6*exp(c7*t)`
Has \(A^2\) and \(e^{A\cdot}\); not linear in \(A\). No log-in-\(t\). Cannot match.  

### 50. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t)`
Has \(A\)-scaled exponential and \(A\) constant term, plus \(A\)-independent exponentials; no \(A\log(\alpha t+1)\). Cannot match.  

---

Because **none** of the candidates can generate the required **\(A\cdot \log(\alpha t+1)\)** dependence (the only log terms depend on \(A\), not \(t\)), no parameter assignment can make any candidate equal the GT for all \(A,t\).

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match

GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_q*A*log(c3*t + c4)

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `0.08820105614498638*A*log(0.4381050266935539*t + 1) - 0.9112380846295999*A*exp(-0.08901020540483869*t)`

The GT has two terms:
1. A term proportional to `A*log(αt + 1)` 
2. A term proportional to `A*exp(-βt)`

Both terms are linear in A. The GT is exactly linear in A (no A², no A^c terms with c≠1, no terms independent of A).

Let me analyze the structure: GT = A * [c_a * log(c_b*t + 1) + c_c * exp(c_d*t)]

This means any matching candidate must be expressible as A times some function of t only, where that function contains both a `log(linear in t)` term and an `exp(linear in t)` term.

Let me check candidates systematically:

**Candidates with A*exp(ct) + A*(constant) structure (linear in A, no log):**
Candidates 1, 4, 7, 8, 19-28, 31-32, 35, 37-39, 42, 48: These have `A*exp(c*t)` and `A*const` terms but NO `A*log(...)` term. The log function cannot be replicated by exponentials and constants. **[NO MATCH]** for all of these.

**Candidates with log terms:**
- **Candidate 2**: Has `c7*log(A*c8 + 1)` - this is log of A, not log of t. [NO MATCH]
- **Candidate 29**: `A*c0 + A*c1 + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*log(A*c6 + 1)` - log of A, not t. [NO MATCH]
- **Candidate 34**: `c4*log(A*c5 + 1)` - log of A. [NO MATCH]
- **Candidate 41**: `c4*log(A*c5 + 1)` - log of A. [NO MATCH]
- **Candidate 44**: `c4*log(A*c5 + 1)` - log of A. [NO MATCH]
- **Candidate 45**: `c5*log(A*c6 + 1)` - log of A. [NO MATCH]

**Candidates with t/(ct+c) structure (could approximate log?):**
- **Candidate 33**: `c4*t/(c5*t + c6) + c7/(c5*t + c6)` = `(c4*t + c7)/(c5*t + c6)`. This is a rational function of t, NOT log. [NO MATCH]
- **Candidate 43**: Similar rational + power terms. [NO MATCH]
- **Candidate 13**: Has `A*c1/(c2*t + c3)` and `c6*log(A*c7 + 1)` - log of A, rational in t. [NO MATCH]

**Candidates with cos, sin, Abs, Max, exp(A*c):** These introduce basis functions not in GT. [NO MATCH] for 3, 5, 6, 9, 10, 11, 12, 14, 15, 16, 17, 18, 23, 30, 36, 40, 46, 47, 49, 50.

**Candidate 8**: Has `c5*t/(c6*t + c7) + c8/(c6*t + c7)` which is rational in t, not log. [NO MATCH]

After checking ALL 50 candidates, none of them contain a term of the form `A*log(c*t + c)`. The GT requires a logarithmic dependence on t multiplied by A, and no candidate provides this structure. Exponentials, rationals, and logs of A cannot replicate `log(t)`.
